============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (PO3)
============================================================
GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*sin(v) - c0*beta*v
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function
\[
f(t,v)=0.106256914230442\,\sin(t)\;-\;0.484396978017638\,\sin(v)\;-\;0.968793956035275\,v.
\]
So it is **additively separable** into a pure \(t\)-term \(A\sin t\) plus a pure \(v\)-term \(-\beta\sin v-2\beta v\). Any matching candidate must be able to produce **both** a \(\sin(t)\) term and simultaneously a \(\sin(v)\) term and a linear-in-\(v\) term (possibly via domain restrictions like \(v\ge 0\) to simplify Abs/Max).

Below, for each candidate, I check whether it can be tuned (constants chosen, and possibly a plausible domain restriction) to equal the GT exactly.

---

### 1. `c0*tanh(c1*t + c2) + c3*exp(c4*cos(c5*t + c6)) + c7*v*Abs(v) + c8*tanh(c9*v)`
- \(t\)-part is tanh and exp(cos), not a pure sine; \(v\)-part is \(v|v|\) and tanh, not \(\sin(v)\) and \(v\).
- You can zero out terms, but you cannot create \(\sin(v)\) or linear \(v\) exactly from these primitives on any nontrivial continuous domain. **No.**

### 2. `c0*v*Max(0, c1 + Abs(v)) + c2 + c3*v + c4*v*Max(0, c5 + Abs(v)) + c6*cos(c7*t + c8)`
- \(t\)-term is cosine; can match \(A\sin t\) via phase shift: set \(c7=1\), \(c8=-\pi/2\), \(c6=A\).
- But \(v\)-dependence is piecewise polynomial/linear via Max/Abs; cannot produce \(-\beta\sin(v)\) exactly on any interval. **No.**

### 3. `... + c4*exp(c5*cos(c6*t + c7))`
- Exponential-of-cos cannot equal a sine function for all \(t\) on an interval unless degenerate constant; then you lose \(\sin(t)\). Also no \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 4. `c0 + c1*exp(c2*t) + c3*exp(c4*sin(c5*t + c6*v + c7))`
- Couples \(t\) and \(v\) inside \(\sin(\cdot)\) unless \(c6=0\). If \(c6=0\), still only exponentials of sin, not linear combination of \(\sin(t)\), \(\sin(v)\), and \(v\). **No.**

### 5. `... + c7*tanh(c8*v)`
- No \(\sin(v)\) and no linear \(v\) (tanh is bounded). **No.**

### 6. `... log(c4*Abs(v) + 1) ... + ... sin(c7*t + c8)`
- Can match \(A\sin t\) by setting the last sine term appropriately and killing other \(t\)-terms.
- But \(v\)-term is \(\log(1+k|v|)\), not \(-\beta\sin v-2\beta v\). **No.**

### 7. `... + c8*v*Max(0, c9 + Abs(v))`
- Again \(v\)-terms are log and piecewise polynomial; no \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 8. `... + c8*v*exp(c9*v**2)/(Abs(v) + 1)`
- No way to equal \(-\beta\sin v-2\beta v\) exactly on an interval. **No.**

### 9. `... + c3*cos(c4*exp(c5*Abs(v))) + c6*sin(c7*t + c8)`
- \(t\)-sine can match \(A\sin t\).
- \(v\)-term is \(\cos(c4 e^{c5|v|})\), not \(\sin(v)\) or linear \(v\). **No.**

### 10. `c0*tanh(...) + c3*exp(c4*cos(c5*t + c6) + c7*v)`
- Couples \(t\) and \(v\) in an exponential unless \(c7=0\) (then no \(v\)-dependence at all). Also cannot yield additive \(-\beta\sin v-2\beta v\). **No.**

### 11. `... + c3*v*exp(c4*v**2) + ... sin(c7*t + c8)`
- \(t\)-sine can match.
- \(v\)-term is \(v e^{c4 v^2}\), not \(\sin(v)+v\). **No.**

### 12. `... + c7*log(c8*exp(c9*v) + 1)`
- Log-sigmoid-like \(v\)-term cannot equal \(-\beta\sin v-2\beta v\) on an interval. **No.**

### 13. `... + c3*v**3 + c4*exp(c5*sin(c6*t + c7))`
- No \(\sin(v)\) and wrong \(t\)-structure (exp(sin)). **No.**

### 14. `... + c7*v**3 + c8*v*Abs(v)`
- No \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 15. Rational in \(t\) plus `exp(c5*Abs(v))*sin(c6*t + c7)`
- The sine term is multiplied by \(e^{c5|v|}\), coupling \(t\) and \(v\). To avoid coupling set \(c5=0\), then you get just \(\sin(c6 t+c7)\) plus rational-in-\(t\), but still no \(\sin(v)\) or linear \(v\). **No.**

### 16. `... + c7*v**3 + c8*v**5`
- No \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 17. `... + c8*v*exp(c9*t)`
- Couples \(t\) and \(v\) unless \(c9=0\) giving linear \(v\). Still no \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 18. `c0*t*exp(c1*t) + c2*exp(c3*t)*sin(c4*t + c5)`
- No \(v\)-dependence at all. **No.**

### 19. `c0/(c1 + t) + c2*v*sin(c3*t + c4) + c5*exp(c6*cos(c7*t + c8) + c9*v)`
- Has \(v\) multiplied by \(\sin(t)\) (coupling) and exponential coupling; cannot become additive separable \(A\sin t + g(v)\) with \(g(v)=-\beta\sin v-2\beta v\) except by killing all \(v\)-terms, which fails. **No.**

### 20. Piecewise linear in \(v\) + `exp(sin(...t+...v...))` + `v*cos(...)`
- No way to get \(\sin(v)\) term; also coupling. **No.**

### 21. Piecewise linear in \(v\) + `exp(sin(t))` + `exp(v)*log(t+1)` coupling
- No \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 22. `... + c8*v` plus other \(t\)-only terms
- You can get the linear \(-0.96879 v\) via \(c8\).
- But there is no \(\sin(v)\) term available. **No.**

### 23. `c0*t/(c1 + c2*exp(c3*t)) + c4*v*Abs(v) + c5*cos(c6*t + c7)*Abs(v)`
- No \(\sin(v)\), and has coupling via \(\cos(t)|v|\). **No.**

### 24. `... + c3*log(...|v|...)*cos(c5*t) + ... + c7*v/(c8*Abs(v) + 1)`
- No \(\sin(v)\). Also coupling via \(\log(|v|)\cos(t)\). **No.**

### 25. Similar to 24 with `v*Max(...)`
- No \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 26. `... + c6*log(c7*Abs(v) + 1)`
- No \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 27. Only Max pieces in \(v\) plus `exp(sin(t))`
- No \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 28. `... + c3*cos(c4*v)*cos(c5*t + c6) + c7*v*cos(c8*t + c9)`
- Contains products coupling \(t\) and \(v\). To remove coupling youŌĆÖd need \(c3=0\) and \(c7=0\), leaving only tanh(t), not \(\sin(t)\). Also no standalone \(\sin(v)\). **No.**

### 29. `... + c4*v*cos(c5*t + c6) + c7*tanh(c8*v)*Max(...)`
